
1a1(ka): / srid pa khams gsum sems can skye 'tshi' mdo zhes bya ba bzhugs so// // 
1b1(ka): g.yung drung lha'i skad du na/
2a1(ka): gu ge sprul ting na ra ha si a a/ bodskad du/ srid pa khams gsum sems
2a2(ka): can skye 'chi yi mdo/ de las gling bzhi'i srid pa phun sum 'tshogs pa'i mdo/ 'di skad
2a3(ka): bdag gis thos pa'i dus cig na/ ston pa gshen rab mi bo ni/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po
2b1(ka): 'jig rten byi thams/ gye lad dkyil ba'i thams/ gzugs tams bcla bdun gyis ta n/ gn rig 'og men bshi sod// dred pa y nga dga po'i sul dang / 
2b2(ka): 'og min lha yi gnas chen dang / bar lha 'od gsal gyi yul khams dang / mgon sum bya yi grong khyer dang bzhi yod de/ 'og men lha'i po brang nas/ s+dzogs sku gnhen lha 
2b3(ka): 'odi dkar gyi/ thugs rje sprul pa'i sku ston pa ghen rab la/ bden pa sum brgya drug tsu' bon rab tu ston te/ thams cad sangs rgyas su gzung pa'i phyir/ sems can 'dren 
2b4(ka): pa de bzhin nyid ces bya ba'i sgom pa chen po mdzad do// de nas sems can de dag gis ston pas ting nge 'dzin de las bzhengs nas/ zang zing med cing mchog tu dga' ba dang / spro 
2b5(ka): ba chen po skyes so// 'jig rten gnhen rab chen po rnams/ mchod pa'i rnam grangs bsam gyis mi khyab pa tsogs nas/ gser gyi khyad par rhad pa'i sprin gyi ba dan sum 
2b6(ka): brgya yis/ soMs kyi dad pa bsam pa stong dang ldan pa dang / g.su ya pad ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'dab ma stong dang ldan pa dang / gsar sum brgya drug cu dang / gsu'i skud pa stong / 
3a1(ka): la ma tog preng ba byas pa dang / glur gum dangosos dang / pad mdbar po dang / pad msngon pa dang / bada ma kha dag du ma sting dang ldan pa dang / rtsi ma gta dang / dpag/ 
3a2(ka): bsam gyi lo ma dang / agse ka dang gser dang / mu teg dang / gsu dang / be du rgya dang / dul dang byu ru dang / ke ke ru dang / rangsa gsi dang / g.su dang shel dang / gser gyi nha dang / 
3a3(ka): g.su'i ma 'dal dang / pad ma sngon po dang / shing star mo ga dang / mhu shel dang / seng ge' gzugs can dang / rgya na dang / zan bya dang / shang teal dang / nha dang glang po che dang / 'd dang 
3a4(ka): nam mkha' ba dan dang / zmang bya'i ldam rgyang dang / rga dang dung dang ghang dang / de dag la stsogs pa/ gnhen rab la mchod pa sprul nas/ 'jig rten khams mi g.yo g.yo med 
3a5(ka): brten pa'i khams zhes bya ba'i mchod pa sul lo// de'i tshe gser ram gsu 'am mchod rten la/ dara sna sum brgya btags nas gnhen rab la mchod pa bul lo// de nas 
3a6(ka): g.sung drung sems dpa' sems dpa'/ brjid pa'i tshul can gyi phyogs bcu nas bzhugs par gyur ta re/ de lta bu'i gnhen rab g.sung dung sems dpa' sems dpa'/ bdud dang / 
3b1(ka): dmyal ba dang / yi dgs dang / me tha ras dang / lha pham lhung can dang / gshin rje'i 'jig nyen pa dang / mi 'am ci dang / srin po'i grong khyer bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang // 
3b2(ka): gnan yang lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyen dang dru za dang / nam ka ldeng dang / grul 'brum dang / 'jig rten pa de dag dam tshig la gnas par bya ba'i phyir/ ston pa gnhen rab mi 
3b3(ka): bi yis/ 'jigs pa'i tshul gyis sku la 'od zer 'bum phrag bye ba phrag khrig 'bum spros pas/ ba spu'i khung bu nas kyang gshen rab bye ba dgu 'bum spros nas/ 'gro ba 
3b4(ka): rnams 'od zer gyi zhags pas bcings nas dbang du bsdus te/ lha 'dre dang / dmu bdud dang / btsan btsun thams cad dam la gnas par bya ba'i phyir/ dam las yongs su gnas 
3b5(ka): par bya ba dang / bde ba'i gnas la drang par bya ba'o// bde ba la gnas par bya ba'i phyir/ ting nge 'dzin gyi znags pas bcing bar bya'o// 'od kyi 'khor los yongs su bstyam par 
3b6(ka): bya'o// 'gro ba sems can yi ge a yi nya la bskyen la/ dbyings nas bstim stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la yongs su bstam par bya'o// stong pa nyid de dag spros pa dang bral ba la / 
4a1(ka): ho/ snoms par 'jug par bya'o/ bde ba la 'jug cing zna'ong gi gnas du m bang par bya ba'i hyir/ ston pa gshen rab kyangsng gi skang brgyad pa bzhi bne bsdol 
4a2(ka): ba'i khri la bzhugs nas/ phyag na sred pa 'od kyi 'khor lo rtsebs stong dang ldan pa bskor nas/ sku gzi brjid dang ldan par byas so// thugs ting nge 'dzin dang ma bral bar/ stong 
4a3(ka): gsum gyi stong chen po 'di zer gyi zhags pas bcings nas/ 'gro ba sems can gang gi khod pa phyogs bcu 'og men du 'khod par byed do// de bzhin du shar phyogs kyi 'jig 
4a4(ka): rten gyi khams gang g klung de na bzhugs par gyur ta ra/ 'das pa kun gyi pha rol na bzhugs pa'i gshen rab/ phyogs bcu dag na sangs rgyas gang dag rnams yon tan rgya 
4a5(ka): mtsho lta bu dag gis/ 'gro ba sems can don byed zhog/ ngas kyang ston pa mi byed gzhan gyi 'dren ston khyed kyang / bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sdong ni khyed kyang bdag gi bstan pa / 
4a6(ka): 'di la gsal gtab tu spyon/ me tog rin chen rin po che/ bdud rtsi rang sa ya na bdug yos chu bo bdud rtsi sman/ mi zad gter dang mar me zhugs thig dang / phye ma phur / 
4b1(ka): mas re lung khyab pa rnams la/ drag cing dtub pa'i sdug bsngal skyon dang sdig sgrib sbyong zhing / bdag la sdong gdab khyed kyang dkyil 'khor 'di la spyin cig/ sems can don ni 
4b2(ka): khyed kyang mdzod cig/ de bzhin du/ byang phyogs kyi 'jig ten gyi khams/ gang ga'i glung de na bzugs par gyur tar/ 'das pa kun gyi pha rol na bzugs pa'i gnhen rab/ 
4b3(ka): phyogs bcu dag na sangs rgyas gang rnams/ yon tan rgya mtsh dag gis 'gro ba sems can don byed zhig/ ngas kyang ston pa mi byed gzhan gyi 'drin ston khyed kyang / bdag gi 
4b4(ka): dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sdong ni khyed kyang / bstan pa 'di la gsal btab rab tu byon/ me tog rin chen rin po che/ bdud rtsi ra sa ya na bdug yis chu bo bdud rtsi sman/ mi zad 
4b5(ka): gter dang mar me zhugs cig dang / phye ma pur mas re lung khyab pa rnams la/ drag cing tsub pa'i sdug bsngal skyon dang sdig sgrib sbyong zhing / bdag la sdong gdab khyed kyang dkyil 
4b6(ka): 'khor 'di la spyon cig/ sems can don ni khyod kyang mdzod cig/ de bzhin du/ thub phyogs kyi 'jig nten gyi khams gang ga'i grlung de na bzhugs par gyur ta r/ 'das pa 
5a1(ka): o/ kun gyi broln bzog pa'i gzheon ob/ phyogs bco dgnasala rgyas rgya btso ni b dag go / 'hro bsem khon don bye zhogg phyi nton pami/ 
5a2(ka): bya/ gnan gyi lden ton khyed byan bdag gdog ba'i ron ni khyed kyang bdagg bstan pa 'di l rab t phyin/ m togin chen ren po ca/ bdu rtse dp yan bdagss
5a3(ka): lu bo bdu rtsi scan/ m zad gter dang mar mi thugs tsog dang / phye ma pur mas ri lung khyab pa rnams la/ drag ci 'lab pa'i sdug bsngal skyon dang sdeg srib byong niang / bdag / 
5a4(ka): la sdong gdab khyed kyang / dkyil 'khor 'di la spyon cig/ sems can don ni khyed kyang mdzoad cig/ de bzhin du lho phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang g klung de na bzhugs 
5a5(ka): par gyur ta r/ 'das pa kun gyi pba rol na bzlugs pa'i/ gzhen rab phyogs bcu dag nas/ sangs rgyas gang rnams yon tan rgya mtsho lta bu dag gis/ 'gro bsems can 
5a6(ka): don byed shig/ ngas kyang ston pa mi kbyed ste/ gzhan gyi 'dren ston khyed kyang / bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sdong ni khyed kyang bdag gi bstan pa 'di la gsal btab rab tu spyon/ 
5b1(ka): me tog rin chen ren po che/ bdud rtsi ran gsa ya na bdug songs chu bo bdud rtsi sman/ mi zad gter dang mar me zhugs tsig dang / phye ma pur mas re lung khyab pa rnams la/ drag 
5b2(ka): cing rub pa'i sdug bsngal skyon dang sdig srib sbyong zhing / bdag la sdong gdab khyed kyang dkyil 'khor 'di na spyon zhing / sems can don ni khyed kyang mdzod cig/ de bzhin du / 
5b3(ka): byang shar gyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang g klung de na bzhugs par gyur ta r/ 'das pa kun gyi pha rol na bzhugs pa'i gnhen rab/ phyogs bcu dag na sangs rgyas gang rnams/ 
5b4(ka): yon tan rgya mtsho lta bu dag gis/ 'gro ba sems can don byed shog/ ngas kyang ston pa mi byed gzhan gyi 'drin ston khyed kyang / bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sdong ni khyed kyang 
5b5(ka): bdag gi bstan pa 'di la gsal btab rab tu spyon/ me tog ren chen ren po che/ bdud rtsi ra s ya na bdug yos chu bo bdud rtsi sman/ mi zad gter dang mar me zhugs 
5b6(ka): thig dang / phye ma pur mas ra lung khyab pa rnams la/ drag cing dtub pa'i sdug bsngal skyon dang sdig sgrib sbyong zhing / bdag la sdong gdab khyed kyang dkyil 'khor 'di na spyon cig/ 
6a1(ka): sems can don ni khyed kyang mdzod cig/ de bzhin du/ byang hub kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang ga'i klung de na bzugs par gyur tar/ 'das pa kun gyi pa rol na /

6a3(ka): gzhan gyi 'dren ston khyed kyang bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sdong ni khyed kyang / bdag gi bstan pa 'di la rab tu spyin/ me togran chen rin po che/ bdud rtsi rangs yana bdug 
6a4(ka): songs chu bo bdud rtsi sman/ mi zad gter dang mar me zhugs thig dang / phye ma phur mas re lung khyab pa rnams la/ drag cing dtrub pa'i sdug bsngal skyon dang sdig sgrib sbyong zhing /

7a1(ka): mas re lung khyab pa rnams la/ drag cing rlab pa'i sdug bsngal skyen dang rdig sgrib byang zhing / bdag la sding gaba khyed kyang dkyil 'khor 'di na spyin zhing / sems

7b5(ka): stsal pa/ ng'i bstan pa'i snying po 'di stong gsum gyi stong chen po 'jig rten gyi khams/ gang ga'i gklung gi bye ba snyed dag na bzugs pa'i ghen rab gsung dung sems dpa' 
7b6(ka): sems dpa' chen po khyed kyis/ bon gyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor/ nyon mongs dug lnga'i rigs rnams bcom par gyur/ sa bcu rgyun gyi tha ma na/ g.yung drung sems dpa' 
8a1(ka): y/ sems dpa'i rgyun ni de ring mthar byin mdzod/ snga ma'i sdig can sems can gyi ni rab kyang 'dren mdzad pa/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i dge ba/ zad pa med pa'i /

8b1(ka): kyis bka' stsal pa/ khyed gsung dung sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams/ gsung drung sems dpa' sems dpa' lam gyi sgron ma can khyed rnams ni/ bskal pa grangs

9a5(ka): du / 'dod chags dang gti mug dangng rgyal dang phrag dog dang lta ba ngan pa dang / tshur rol pa dang / pha rol dang / rtogs pa dang sems can dang / srog dang las ngan pa dang / sgrib pa thams

9b6(ka): gshen rab kyis 'dul zhing chen po dang ldan pa'i bon bshad pa 'di dam bcas pas/ gnhen rab g.yung dung sems dpa' rab tu 'dren par byed do// sdig po che la sogs pa'i bdud 
10a1(ka): dang / ce ma yin dang / bha bzen dang / de zadng gzhin rje d brul bam dang / dmyal badang ma dgs d khyil'i dang / me 'khad nam mtha' he dang / ga da/

10a5(ka): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lam gyi sgron mas gsol pa/ bdag gi lag pa gnyis na yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che tsogs nas/ gsung dung sems dpa' sems dpa' 
10a6(ka): chen po dbyangs dang ldan pa de la 'di skad ces gsol pa/ g.yung drung sems dpa' sems dpa' lam gyi sgron ma can khyed kyis/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'di'i sems can ni/ 
10b1(ka): 'bru 'am srang bu'i rigs dang gang yin par mthong nas/ ngas snying rje ba'i bsam pa mang po skyes nas/ sems can thams cad ni du 'bod dang bsad pa dang / gcad pa dang / brtung dang 
10b2(ka): brteg pa dang / btags pa dang 'dzin pa dang / de dag sems can dmyal ba'i las de kun/ bde ba'i po brang du skye bar 'gyur bar 'dod pa'i phyir/ de bzhin du/ zhe sdang dang gti bug 
10b3(ka): dang / 'dod chags dang / nga rgyal dang phrag dog yod pas/ ming gi dngos po ni rkyen gyi mtshan nyid do// mtshan nyid kyi rkyen ni ma rig pa'o// ma rig pa'i rkyen ni 'du byed rnams/ 
10b4(ka): 'gog pa'i bar du rgyas par bya'o// gsol pa/ g.sung dung sems dpa' sems dpa' lam gyi sgron ma can gyis gsol pa/ ma rig pa zhes gsungs pa/ gnhen rab ma rig pa
